 ProfileObservation,\n    ProfileUpdate,\n    UserProfile,\n)\n\n\nclass ProfileService:\n    \"\"\"Service for managing user profiles.\n\n    TODO: Replace in-memory storage with Neo4j persistence.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Initialize with in-memory storage for now.\"\"\"\n        self._profiles: dict[str, UserProfile] = {}\n\n    async def get_profile(self, user_id: str) -> UserProfile | None:\n        \"\"\"Get profile by user ID.\"\"\"\n        return self._profiles.get(user_id)\n\n    async def create_profile(\n        self, user_id: str, display_name: str | None = None\n    ) -> UserProfile:\n        \"\"\"Create a new profile with defaults.\"\"\"\n        profile = UserProfile(\n            user_id=user_id,\n            display_name=display_name,\n            last_updated=datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),\n        )\n        self._profiles[user_id] = profile\n        return profile\n\n    async def update_profile(\n        self, user_id: str, update: ProfileUpdate\n    ) -> UserProfile | None:\n        \"\"\"Update profile dimensions.\"\"\"\n        profile = self._profiles.get(user_id)\n        if not profile:\n            return None\n\n        update_data = update.model_dump(exclude_unset=True)\n        for field, value in update_data.items():\n            if value is not None:\n                setattr(profile, field, value)\n\n        profile.last_updated = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()\n        self._profiles[user_id] = profile\n        return profile\n\n    async def record_capacity(\n        self, user_id: str, check_in: CapacityCheckIn\n    ) -> UserProfile | None:\n        \"\"\"Record capacity check-in.\"\"\"\n        profile = self._profiles.get(user_id)\n        if not profile:\n            return None\n\n        profile.attention.current_capacity = check_in.current_capacity\n        profile.last_updated = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()\n        self._profiles[user_id] = profile\n        return profile\n\n    async def apply_observation(\n        self, user_id: str, observation: ProfileObservation\n    ) -> UserProfile | None:\n        \"\"\"Apply session observations to update profile.\n\n        This is where the system learns about the user over time.\n        \"\"\"\n        profile = self._profiles.get(user_id)\n        if not profile:\n            return None\n\n        # Increment session count\n        profile.sessions_completed += 1\n\n        # Update hyperfocus triggers if new topics engaged deeply\n        for topic in observation.topics_explored:\n            if topic not in profile.attention.hyperfocus_triggers:\n                # TODO: Only add if session showed deep engagement\n                pass\n\n        # Track approach effectiveness for future question selection\n        # TODO: Store this in a separate analytics structure\n\n        profile.last_updated = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()\n        self._profiles[user_id] = profile\n        return profile\n\n    async def get_profile_summary(self, user_id: str) -> dict | None:\n        \"\"\"Get condensed profile summary for session context.\n\n        Returns a prompt-friendly summary of key profile dimensions.\n        \"\"\"\n        profile = self._profiles.get(user_id)\n        if not profile:\n            return None\n\n        return {\n            \"user_id\": profile.user_id,\n            \"display_name\": profile.display_name,\n            \"current_capacity\": profile.attention.current_capacity,\n            \"optimal_session_length\": profile.attention.optimal_session_length,\n            \"processing_style\": profile.processing.style.value,\n            \"pace_preference\": profile.communication.pace.value,\n            \"directness\": profile.communication.directness_preference,\n            \"structure_need\": profile.executive.structure_need.value,\n            \"hyperfocus_triggers\": profile.attention.hyperfocus_triggers[:5],\n            \"overwhelm_signals\": profile.sensory.overwhelm_signals[:3],\n            \"sessions_completed\": profile.sessions_completed,\n            \"onboarding_complete\": profile.onboarding_complete,\n        }\n"

    "input": {
      "file_path": "/home/chris/dev/projects/codex/brain_explore/.claude/commands/onboard-profile.md",
      "content": "# IES Profile Onboarding\n\nYou are guiding the user through building their **cognitive profile** — a map of how their brain works that will personalize all future exploration sessions.\n\n## Purpose\n\nThis profile helps IES adapt to your unique:\n- **Processing style** — how you take in and organize information\n- **Attention patterns** — what captures your focus, what depletes you\n- **Communication preferences** — pace, directness, structure needs\n- **Executive functioning** — task initiation, transitions, working memory\n- **Sensory needs** — environment, overwhelm signals\n\n## Conversation Style\n\n**Be conversational, not clinical.** This isn't a diagnostic assessment — it's a curious exploration of how the user's brain works. Use their language, not clinical jargon.\n\n**One dimension at a time.** Don't overwhelm with all questions at once. Explore naturally.\n\n**Validate neurodivergent experiences.** Many profile dimensions are ADHD/autism-relevant. Frame differences as adaptations, not deficits.\n\n**Use examples.** Abstract questions are hard. Ground them: \"When you're working on something you love, do you lose track of time? Or do you stay aware of the clock?\"\n\n## Onboarding Flow\n\n### 1. Opening (set context)\n\nStart with something like:\n> \"Let's build a map of how your brain works. This helps me adapt how I ask questions, pace conversations, and support your thinking. There are no wrong answers — just curiosity about your patterns.\n>\n> We'll explore a few dimensions: how you process information, what captures your attention, how you like to communicate, and what helps you do your best thinking.\n>\n> Ready to start?\"\n\n### 2. Processing Style\n\nExplore:\n- **Detail-first vs pattern-first**: \"When you encounter something new, do you tend to notice the specific details first? Or do you jump to the big picture and fill in details later?\"\n- **Deliberative vs intuitive**: \"When making decisions, do you prefer to think through options systematically? Or do you often 'just know' what feels right?\"\n- **Abstraction level**: \"Do you prefer concrete examples or theoretical frameworks?\"\n\n### 3. Attention & Energy\n\nExplore:\n- **Hyperfocus triggers**: \"What kinds of topics or activities can totally absorb you? Where time disappears?\"\n- **Distraction patterns**: \"What typically pulls you away from what you're doing?\"\n- **Energy recovery**: \"When you're mentally tired, what helps you recharge?\"\n- **Session length**: \"How long can you typically stay engaged in deep conversation before needing a break?\"\n\n### 4. Communication Preferences\n\nExplore:\n- **Verbal fluency**: \"How easily do words come when you're thinking out loud? Easy flow, or sometimes searching for the right words?\"\n- **Pace**: \"Do you prefer rapid back-and-forth or more space between exchanges?\"\n- **Directness**: \"Do you prefer gentle questions or direct challenges?\"\n- **Wait time**: \"Do you need time to process before responding, or do you think as you speak?\"\n\n### 5. Executive Functioning\n\nExplore:\n- **Task initiation**: \"Starting things — easy, hard, or depends on the thing?\"\n- **Transitions**: \"How hard is it to switch from one task or topic to another?\"\n- **Structure needs**: \"Do you prefer clear structure or flexible exploration?\"\n- **Working memory**: \"If I mention three things, will you remember them later? Or should I circle back?\"\n\n### 6. Sensory Context (optional, if natural)\n\nExplore:\n- **Environment**: \"What kind of environment helps you think best?\"\n- **Overwhelm signals**: \"How do you know when you're getting overwhelmed? Any early warning signs?\"\n- **Regulation tools**: \"What helps you get back to a good thinking state?\"\n\n### 7. Closing\n\nSummarize what you learned:\n> \"Based on our conversation, here's what I'm taking away about how your brain works:\n> [Summary in their language, highlighting key patterns]\n>\n> Does that feel accurate? Anything you'd adjust?\"\n\n## After Onboarding\n\nWhen onboarding is complete:\n\n1. **Create profile JSON** — Generate the profile structure based on the conversation\n2. **Save to backend** — POST to `/profile/{user_id}` endpoint\n3. **Note in progress file** — Record that onboarding was completed\n4. **Explain next steps** — \"Your profile is saved. Future sessions will adapt to these patterns. You can always update it later.\"\n\n## Profile Schema Reference\n\n```json\n{\n  \"processing\": {\n    \"style\": \"detail_first | pattern_first | balanced\",\n    \"decision_style\": \"deliberative | intuitive | mixed\",\n    \"habituation_speed\": 1-10,\n    \"abstraction_preference\": 1-10\n  },\n  \"attention\": {\n    \"hyperfocus_triggers\": [\"list of topics/contexts\"],\n    \"distraction_vulnerabilities\": [\"list\"],\n    \"current_capacity\": 1-10,\n    \"recovery_patterns\": [\"list\"],\n    \"optimal_session_length\": 5-120 minutes\n  },\n  \"communication\": {\n    \"verbal_fluency\": 1-10,\n    \"scripts_preference\": 1-10,\n    \"directness_preference\": 1-10,\n    \"pace\": \"fast | slow | adaptive\",\n    \"wait_time_needed\": 1-10\n  },\n  \"executive\": {\n    \"task_initiation\": 1-10,\n    \"transition_cost\": 1-10,\n    \"time_perception\": 1-10,\n    \"structure_need\": \"rigid | flexible | moderate\",\n    \"working_memory\": 1-10\n  },\n  \"sensory\": {\n    \"environment_preference\": 1-10,\n    \"overwhelm_signals\": [\"list\"],\n    \"regulation_tools\": [\"list\"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n## Do NOT\n\n- Rush through dimensions\n- Use clinical language unless user does\n- Frame neurodivergent traits as problems\n- Skip the summary/verification step\n- Forget to save the profile\n\nBegin by introducing the onboarding purpose and asking if the user is ready.\n"
    }
  }

\"\"\"Client for SiYuan API interactions.\"\"\"\n\n    @classmethod\n    def _get_base_url(cls) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get the SiYuan API base URL.\"\"\"\n        return f\"http://{settings.siyuan_host}:{settings.siyuan_port}\"\n\n    @classmethod\n    def _get_headers(cls) -> dict[str, str]:\n        \"\"\"Get request headers with auth token.\"\"\"\n        return {\n            \"Authorization\": f\"Token {settings.siyuan_token}\",\n            \"Content-Type\": \"application/json\",\n        }\n\n    @classmethod\n    async def _request(\n        cls, endpoint: str, data: dict[str, Any] | None = None\n    ) -> dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Make a request to the SiYuan API.\"\"\"\n        async with httpx.AsyncClient() as client:\n            response = await client.post(\n                f\"{cls._get_base_url()}/api{endpoint}\",\n                headers=cls._get_headers(),\n                json=data or {},\n                timeout=30.0,\n            )\n            response.raise_for_status()\n            result = response.json()\n            if result.get(\"code\") != 0:\n                raise Exception(f\"SiYuan API error: {result.get('msg')}\")\n            return result.get(\"data\", {})\n\n    @classmethod\n    async def create_doc(\n        cls, notebook: str, path: str, markdown: str\n    ) -> dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Create a new document in SiYuan.\n\n        Args:\n            notebook: Notebook ID\n            path: Document path (e.g., \"/Profiles/chris\")\n            markdown: Markdown content\n\n        Returns:\n            Document info including ID\n        \"\"\"\n        return await cls._request(\n            \"/filetree/createDocWithMd\",\n            {\"notebook\": notebook, \"path\": path, \"markdown\": markdown},\n        )\n\n    @classmethod\n    async def update_block(cls, block_id: str, markdown: str) -> dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Update a block's content.\n\n        Args:\n            block_id: Block ID to update\n            markdown: New markdown content\n        \"\"\"\n        return await cls._request(\n            \"/block/updateBlock\",\n            {\"id\": block_id, \"data\": markdown, \"dataType\": \"markdown\"},\n        )\n\n    @classmethod\n    async def get_block_kramdown(cls, block_id: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Get a block's kramdown source.\"\"\"\n        result = await cls._request(\"/block/getBlockKramdown\", {\"id\": block_id})\n        return result.get(\"kramdown\", \"\")\n\n    @classmethod\n    async def sql_query(cls, sql: str) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"Execute a SQL query against SiYuan's database.\n\n        Args:\n            sql: SQL query string\n\n        Returns:\n            List of matching records\n        \"\"\"\n        result = await cls._request(\"/query/sql\", {\"stmt\": sql})\n        return result if isinstance(result, list) else []\n\n    @classmethod\n    async def ID\n            path: Human-readable path (e.g., \"/Profiles/chris\")\n\n        Returns:\n            Document info or None if not found\n        \"\"\"\n        # Get IDs by hpath\n        try:\n            result = await cls._request(\n                \"/filetree/getIDsByHPath\",\n                {\"notebook\": notebook, \"path\": path},\n            )\n            if result:\n                return {\"id\": result[0]} if isinstance(result, list) else {\"id\": result}\n        except Exception:\n            pass\n        return None\n\n    @classmethod\n    async def append_block(\n        cls, parent_id: str, markdown: str\n    ) -> dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Append a block as a child of the given parent.\n\n        Args:\n            parent_id: Parent block ID\n       "file_path": "/home/chris/dev/projects/codex/brain_explore/ies-backend/src/ies_backend/services/siyuan_profile_service.py",
      "content": "\"\"\"SiYuan profile page service - creates human-readable profile pages.\"\"\"\n\nfrom ies_backend.schemas.profile import UserProfile\nfrom ies_backend.services.siyuan_client import SiYuanClient\n\n\nclass SiYuanProfileService:\n    \"\"\"Service for managing profile pages in SiYuan.\"\"\"\n\n    # Default notebook for IES profiles\n    DEFAULT_NOTEBOOK = \"20241201000000-ies\"  # Will be configured\n\n    def __init__(self, notebook_id: str | None = None):\n        \"\"\"Initialize with optional notebook override.\"\"\"\n        self.notebook_id = notebook_id or self.DEFAULT_NOTEBOOK\n\n    async def create_or_update_profile_page(self, profile: UserProfile) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Create or update a profile page in SiYuan.\n\n        Args:\n            profile: User profile to render\n\n        Returns:\n            Document ID\n        \"\"\"\n        markdown = self._render_profile_markdown(profile)\n        path = f\"/Profiles/{profile.user_id}\"\n\n        # Check if page exists\n        existing = await SiYuanClient.find_doc_by_path(self.notebook_id, path)\n\n        if existing:\n            # Update existing page\n            await SiYuanClient.update_block(existing[\"id\"], markdown)\n            return existing[\"id\"]\n        else:\n            # Create new page\n            result = await SiYuanClient.create_doc(\n                self.notebook_id, path, markdown\n            )\n            return result.get(\"id\", \"\")\n\n    def _render_profile_markdown(self, profile: UserProfile) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Render profile as human-readable markdown.\"\"\"\n        lines = [\n            f\"# {profile.display_name or profile.user_id}'s Profile\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"*Last updated: {profile.last_updated or 'Never'}*\",\n            \"\",\n        ]\n\n        # Processing Style\n        lines.extend([\n            \"## Processing Style\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"- **Information processing**: {self._format_style(profile.processing.style.value)}\",\n            f\"- **Decision making**: {self._format_style(profile.processing.decision_style.value)}\",\n            f\"- **Habituation speed**: {self._format_scale(profile.processing.habituation_speed, 'slow to habituate', 'quick to habituate')}\",\n            f\"- **Abstraction preference**: {self._format_scale(profile.processing.abstraction_preference, 'concrete examples', 'theoretical frameworks')}\",\n            \"\",\n        ])\n\n        # Attention & Energy\n        lines.extend([\n            \"## Attention & Energy\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"- **Current capacity**: {profile.attention.current_capacity}/10\",\n            f\"- **Optimal session length**: {profile.attention.optimal_session_length} minutes\",\n            \"\",\n        ])\n\n        if profile.attention.hyperfocus_triggers:\n            lines.append(\"**Hyperfocus triggers:**\")\n            for trigger in profile.attention.hyperfocus_triggers:\n                lines.append(f\"- {trigger}\")\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        if profile.attention.distraction_vulnerabilities:\n            lines.append(\"**Distraction vulnerabilities:**\")\n            for vuln in profile.attention.distraction_vulnerabilities:\n                lines.append(f\"- {vuln}\")\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        if profile.attention.recovery_patterns:\n            lines.append(\"**Recovery patterns:**\")\n            for pattern in profile.attention.recovery_patterns:\n                lines.append(f\"- {pattern}\")\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        # Communication\n        lines.extend([\n            \"## Communication Preferences\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"- **Verbal fluency**: {self._format_scale(profile.communication.verbal_fluency, 'searching for words', 'easy flow')}\",\n            f\"- **Pace preference**: {profile.communication.pace.value}\",\n            f\"- **Directness**: {self._format_scale(profile.communication.directness_preference, 'gentle', 'direct')}\",\n            f\"- **Wait time needed**: {self._format_scale(profile.communication.wait_time_needed, 'thinks while speaking', 'needs processing time')}\",\n            \"\",\n        ])\n\n        # Executive Functioning\n        lines.extend([\n            \"## Executive Functioning\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"- **Task initiation**: {self._format_scale(profile.executive.task_initiation, 'hard to start', 'easy to start')}\",\n            f\"- **Transition cost**: {self._format_scale(profile.executive.transition_cost, 'easy switches', 'high switching cost')}\",\n            f\"- **Time perception**: {self._format_scale(profile.executive.time_perception, 'time aware', 'time blind')}\",\n            f\"- **Structure need**: {profile.executive.structure_need.value}\",\n            f\"- **Working memory**: {self._format_scale(profile.executive.working_memory, 'limited', 'strong')}\",\n            \"\",\n        ])\n\n        # Sensory\n        lines.extend([\n            \"## Sensory & Environment\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"- **Environment preference**: {self._format_scale(profile.sensory.environment_preference, 'quiet', 'stimulating')}\",\n            \"\",\n        ])\n\n        if profile.sensory.overwhelm_signals:\n            lines.append(\"**Overwhelm signals:**\")\n            for signal in profile.sensory.overwhelm_signals:\n                lines.append(f\"- {signal}\")\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        if profile.sensory.regulation_tools:\n            lines.append(\"**Regulation tools:**\")\n            for tool in profile.sensory.regulation_tools:\n                lines.append(f\"- {tool}\")\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        # Metadata\n        lines.extend([\n            \"---\",\n            \"\",\n            \"## Session History\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"- **Sessions completed**: {profile.sessions_completed}\",\n            f\"- **Onboarding complete**: {'Yes' if profile.onboarding_complete else 'No'}\",\n        ])\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n\n    def _format_style(self, value: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Format enum style values for display.\"\"\"\n        return value.replace(\"_\", \" \").title()\n\n    def _format_scale(self, value: int, low_label: str, high_label: str) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Format a 1-10 scale value with labels.\"\"\"\n        if value <= 3:\n            return f\"{value}/10 ({low_label})\"\n        elif value >= 8:\n            return f\"{value}/10 ({high_label})\"\n        else:\n            return f\"{value}/10 (moderate)\"\n"
    }
  }

It enables Socratic questioning that adapts to the user's cognitive profile, captures insights as entities, and builds a knowledge graph connecting personal understanding with research literature.\n    11→\n    12→**Key Insight:** The conversation engine itself is the core of IES, not just a passthrough to extraction. Conversations must be correctly focused, structured, and guided based on how the user's brain works.\n    13→\n    14→---\n    15→\n    16→## Architecture Summary\n    17→\n    18→```\n    19→┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n    20→│                     CLAUDE CODE                                      │\n    21→│                                                                      │\n    22→│  /explore-session                                                    │\n    23→│       ↓                                                              │\n    24→│  Profile-informed Socratic conversation                              │\n    25→│       ↓                                                              │\n    26→│  /end-session                                                        │\n    27→│       ↓                                                              │\n    28→│  Transcript captured → sent to backend                               │\n    29→└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n    30→                            ↓\n    31→┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n    32→│                     BACKEND (FastAPI)                                │\n    33→│                                                                      │\n    34→│  1. Receive transcript                                               │\n    35→│  2. Extract entities (Claude API)                                    │\n    36→│  3. Generate structured session document                             │\n    39→│  6. Profile System\n    49→\n    50→### Purpose\n    51→\n    52→Understand the user's brain and thinking patterns to create personalized exploration strategies. The profile shapes how conversations are approached—not just what topics are discussed.\n    53→\n    54→### Profile Dimensions\n    55→\n    56→```\n    57→1. Processing Style\n    58→   - Detail-first ←→ Pattern-first\n    59→   - Deliberative ←→ Intuitive\n    60→   - Habituation speed (how quickly \"new\" becomes \"familiar\")\n    61→\n    62→2. Attention & Energy\n    63→   - Hyperfocus triggers (what topics/contexts unlock flow)\n    64→   - Distraction vulnerabilities\n    65→   - Current capacity (daily/session check-in)\n    66→   - Recovery patterns (what restores energy)\n    67→\n    68→3. Communication Preferences\n    69→   - Verbal fluency level\n    70→   - Scripts vs spontaneity preference\n    71→   - Directness preference\n    72→   - Pace (fast exchange vs slow reflection)\n    73→\n    74→4. Executive Functioning\n    75→   - Task initiation patterns\n    76→   - Transition costs\n    77→   - Time perception\n    78→   - Structure needs (rigid ←→ flexible)\n    79→\n    80→5. Sensory Context\n    81→   - Environment preferences (quiet/stimulating)\n    82→   - Overwhelm signals\n    83→   - Regulation tools that help\n    84→\n    85→6. Masking Awareness (optional/advanced)\n    86→   - What traits feel unsafe to show\n    87→   - Energy cost of different contexts\n    88→```\n    89→\n    90→### Onboarding Approach\n    91→\n    92→**Not a formal assessment battery** — that's clinical. Instead:\n    93→\n    94→1. **Conversational intake** (2-3 sessions) — AI asks questions drawn from assessment frameworks, but conversationally\n    95→2. **Observation-based refinement** — System notes patterns during regular sessions\n    96→3. **User self-report** — \"Today I'm at 60% capacity\" type check-ins\n    97→4. **Explicit profile review** — Periodic \"does this still feel accurate?\"\n    98→\n    99→### Research Foundation\n   100→\n   101→Profile dimensions drawn from:\n   102→- Barkley ADHD/Executive Function scales (19 assessments in Neo4j)\n   103→- Devon Price's \"Unmasking Autism\" (masking, contextual functioning)\n   104→- Beck instruments (mood/anxiety baseline)\n   105→- Big Five personality model (cognitive style)\n   106→\n   107→---\n   108→\n   109→## 2. Question Design Engine\n   110→\n   111→### Purpose\n   112→\n   113→Dynamically select questioning approaches based on user state, content type, and profile—not just default Socratic questioning.\n   114→\n   115→### Inquiry Approaches (from resources)\n   116→\n   117→| Approach | When to Use |\n   118→|----------|-------------|\n   119→| **Socratic** | Stuck in loops, need clarity |\n   120→| **Metacognitive** | Need clarity, reflection on thinking |\n   121→| **Phenomenological / Focusing** | Emotion-heavy, body-based knowing |\n   122→| **CBT** | Stuck in loops, testing beliefs |\n   123→| **Solution-focused** | Overwhelmed, need forward motion |\n   124→| **Systems thinking** | Unclear purpose, meaning-making |\n   125→| **Design thinking** | Unclear purpose, problem reframing |\n   126→| **Narrative** | Emotion-heavy, meaning-making |\n   127→| **Strategic** | Planning, decision-making |\n   128→| **Somatic** | Overwhelmed, grounding needed |\n   129→\n   130→### Selection Logic\n   131→\n   132→```\n   133→DETECT STATE\n   134→    ↓\n   135→├─ Overwhelmed? → Solution-focused, Somatic\n   136→├─ Stuck in loops? → Socratic, CBT\n   137→├─ Unclear purpose? → Design thinking, Systems\n   138→├─ Emotion-heavy? → Phenomenological, Narrative\n   139→├─ Need clarity? → Metacognitive, Socratic\n   140→├─ Planning mode? → Strategic inquiry\n   141→└─ Meaning-making? → Narrative, Systems\n   142→    ↓\n   143→SELECT APPROACH → APPLY TOOLS/TEMPLATES\n   144→```\n   145→\n   146→### MVP Scope\n   147→\n   148→Start with 4-5 core approaches:\n   149→1. **Socratic** — core default\n   150→2. **Solution-focused** — when overwhelmed\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. Session Flow\n   170→\n   171→### Lifecycle\n   172→\n   173→```\n   174→1. SESSION START\n   175→   ├── Load user profile\n   176→   ├── Check current capacity (\"How are you feeling? 1-10\")\n   177→   ├── Load recent session context (last topics, open threads)\n   178→   └── AI proposes starting point based on profile + state\n   179→\n   180→2. EXPLORATION LOOP\n   181→   ┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n   182→   │  DETECT STATE                                           │\n   183→   │  ├── Energy level (from responses, length, tone)        │\n   184→   │  ├── Cognitive state (overwhelmed, stuck, flowing)      │\n   185→   │  └── Content type (abstract, emotional, concrete)       │\n   186→   │                        ↓                                │\n   187→   │  SELECT APPROACH (from question engine)                 │\n   188→   │                        ↓                                │\n   189→   │  ASK QUESTION (adapted to profile)                      │\n   190→   │  ├── Pacing (fast/slow per profile)                     │\n   191→   │  ├── Abstraction level (concrete/theoretical)           │\n   192→   │  └── Directness (blunt/gentle)                          │\n   193→   │                        ↓                                │\n   194→   │  PROCESS RESPONSE                                       │\n   195→   │  ├── Note entities emerging                             │\n   196→   │  ├── Track thread (what we're exploring)                │\n   197→   │  └── Update state detection                             │\n   198→   └─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n   199→                    ↓ (repeat until pause signal)\n   200→\n   201→3. SESSION END\n   202→   ├── Detect pause signal (energy dip, explicit, natural end)\n   203→   ├── AI summarizes session\n   204→   ├── User confirms/edits summary\n   205→   └── Trigger backend extraction\n   206→\n   207→4. POST-SESSION (Backend)\n   208→   ├── Extract entities from transcript\n   209→   ├── Create structured session document in SiYuan\n   210→   ├── Create/update entity pages\n   211→   ├── Update Neo4j graph\n   212→   └── Update profile (patterns observed)\n   213→```\n   214→\n   215→### Profile Influence Points\n   216→\n   217→| Profile Dimension | How It Affects Session |\n   218→|-------------------|------------------------|\n   219→| Processing style | Question sequence, abstraction level |\n   220→| Attention patterns | Topic steering, depth vs breadth |\n   221→| Current capacity | Session length, complexity |\n   222→| Communication preference | Question phrasing, wait time |\n   223→| Sensory/energy context | Pause frequency, break suggestions |\n   224→\n   225→---\n   226→\n   227→## 4. Entity System\n   228→\n   229→### Light Schema\n   230→\n   231→```\n   232→kind: idea | person | process | question | tension\n   233→domain: therapy | personal | meta\n   234→status: seed | developing | solid\n   235→```\n   236→\n   237→Connections and tags do the rest of the work. Ontology emerges from use, not defined upfront.\n   238→\n   239→### Extraction Schema (Claude prompt output)\n   240→\n   241→```json\n   242→{\n   243→  \"entities\": [\n   244→    {\n   245→      \"name\": \"string\",\n   246→      \"kind\": \"idea | person | process | question | tension\",\n   247→      \"domain\": \"therapy | personal | meta\",\n   248→      \"status\": \"seed | developing | solid\",\n   249→      \"description\": \"string\",\n   250→      \"quotes\": [\"exact quotes from transcript\"],\n   251→      \"connections\": [\n   252→        {\"to\": \"entity_name\", \"relationship\": \"supports | tensions | develops\"}\n   253→      ]\n   254→    }\n   255→  ],\n   256→  \"session_summary\": {\n   257→    \"key_insights\": [\"string\"],\n   258→    \"open_questions\": [\"string\"],\n   259→    \"threads_explored\": [\"string\"]\n   260→  }\n   261→}\n   262→```\n   263→\n   264→### Session Document Structure\n   265→\n   266→Structured sections (not chronological transcript):\n   267→- **Key Insights** — What emerged\n   268→- **Entities Discussed** — With status and connections\n   269→- **Open Questions** — Unresolved threads\n   270→- **Key Quotes** — Important moments\n   271→- **Context** — Enough to remember what you were thinking\n   272→\n   273→Raw transcript stored separately if needed.\n   274→\n   275→---\n   276→\n   277→## 5. Backend Architecture\n   278→\n   279→### Tech Stack\n   280→\n   281→| Component | Technology | Purpose |\n   282→|-----------|------------|---------|\n   283→| API Framework | FastAPI | Async, streaming support |\n   284→| Graph Database | Neo4j | Entities, relations, profile queries |\n   285→| Vector Store | Qdrant | Semantic search (existing) |\n   286→| Document Store | SiYuan | Human-readable pages |\n   287→| LLM | Claude API | Entity extraction, summaries |\n   288→\n   289→### Endpoints\n   290→\n   291→```\n   292→POST /session/process\n   293→├── Input: transcript, user_id\n   294→├── Extract entities (Claude API)\n   295→├── Generate session document\n   296→├── Create/update entity pages (SiYuan API)\n   297→├── Update graph (Neo4j)\n   298→└── Output: session_doc_id, entities_created, entities_updated\n   299→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. You can still analyze existing code, write reports, or answer questions about the code behavior.\n</system-reminder>\n"

ies_backend.schemas.entity import (\n    EntityConnection,\n    EntityDomain,\n    EntityKind,\n    EntityStatus,\n    ExtractionResult,\n    ExtractedEntity,\n    SessionSummary,\n)\n\n\nEXTRACTION_PROMPT = \"\"\"You are an expert at identifying and extracting knowledge entities from exploratory conversations.\n\nAnalyze the following transcript and extract:\n\n1. **Entities** - Ideas, concepts, questions, tensions, people, or processes that emerged\n2. **Connections** - How entities relate to each other\n3. **Session Summary** - Key insights, open questions, and threads explored\n\nFor each entity, determine:\n- **kind**: idea | person | process | question | tension\n  - idea: A concept, belief, or insight\n  - person: A theorist, author, or figure referenced\n  - process: A method, technique, or way of doing something\n  - question: An open question or inquiry\n  - tension: A conflict, paradox, or unresolved opposition\n\n- **domain**: therapy | personal | meta\n  - therapy: Related to therapeutic approach, theory, or practice\n  - personal: Related to the user's personal experience or context\n  - meta: About the exploration process itself\n\n- **status**: seed | developing | solid\n  - seed: First mention, rough idea, needs more exploration\n  - developing: Has been explored some, taking shape\n  - solid: Well-developed, clearly articulated\n\n- **connections**: How this entity relates to others\n  - supports: This entity supports/strengthens another\n  - tensions: This entity is in tension with another\n  - develops: This entity develops/extends another\n\nExtract exact quotes from the transcript that support each entity.\n\nTRANSCRIPT:\n{transcript}\n\nRespond with valid JSON matching this schema:\n{{\n  \"entities\": [\n    {{\n      \"name\": \"string\",\n      \"kind\": \"idea | person | process | question | tension\",\n      \"domain\": \"therapy | personal | meta\",\n      \"status\": \"seed | developing | solid\",\n      \"description\": \"string\",\n      \"quotes\": [\"exact quotes from transcript\"],\n      \"connections\": [\n        {{\"to\": \"entity_name\", \"relationship\": \"supports | tensions | develops\"}}\n      ]\n    }}\n  ],\n  \"session_summary\": {{\n    \"key_insights\": [\"string\"],\n    \"open_questions\": [\"string\"],\n    \"threads_explored\": [\"string\"]\n  }}\n}}\n\nBe selective - only extract meaningful entities that represent genuine insights, not every topic mentioned.\nPrefer fewer, richer entities over many shallow ones.\"\"\"\n\n\nclass ExtractionService:\n    \"\"\"Service for extracting entities from session transcripts using Claude.\"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(self) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Initialize with Anthropic client.\"\"\"\n        self.client = AsyncAnthropic(api_key=settings.anthropic_api_key)\n\n    async def extract_entities(self, transcript: str) -> ExtractionResult:\n        \"\"\"Extract entities and summary from a transcript.\n\n        Args:\n            transcript: Raw session transcript\n\n        Returns:\n            ExtractionResult with entities and summary\n        \"\"\"\n        prompt = EXTRACTION_PROMPT.format(transcript=transcript)\n\n        message = await self.client.messages.create(\n            model=\"claude-sonnet-4-20250514\",\n            max_tokens=4096,\n            messages=[\n                {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}\n            ],\n        )\n\n        # Parse response\n        response_text = message.content[0].text\n\n        # Extract JSON from response (handle markdown code blocks)\n        json_text = response_text\n        if \"```json\" in json_text:\n            json_text = json_text.split(\"```json\")[1].split(\"```\")[0]\n        elif \"```\" in json_text:\n            json_text = json_text.split(\"```\")[1].split(\"```\")[0]\n\n        try:\n            data = json.loads(json_text.strip())\n        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:\n            # If parsing fails, return empty result\n            return ExtractionResult(\n                entities=[],\n                session_summary=SessionSummary(\n                    key_insights=[f\"Extraction failed: {str(e)}\"],\n                    open_questions=[],\n                    threads_explored=[],\n                ),\n            )\n\n        # Convert to Pydantic models\n        entities = []\n        for entity_data in data.get(\"entities\", []):\n            try:\n                connections = [\n                    EntityConnection(\n                        to=conn[\"to\"],\n                        relationship=conn[\"relationship\"],\n                    )\n                    for conn in entity_data.get(\"connections\", [])\n                ]\n\n                entity = ExtractedEntity(\n                    name=entity_data[\"name\"],\n description=entity_data[\"description\"],\n                    quotes=entity_data.get(\"quotes\", []),\n                    connections=connections,\n                )\n                entities.append(entity)\n            except (KeyError, ValueError):\n                # Skip malformed entities\n                continue\n\n        summary_data = data.get(\"session_summary\", {})\n        summary = SessionSummary(\n            key_insights=summary_data.get(\"key_insights\", []),\n            open_questions=summary_data.get(\"open_questions\", []),\n            threads_explored=summary_data.get(\"threads_explored\", []),\n        )\n\n        return ExtractionResult(entities=entities, session_summary=summary)\n"

      "content": "\"\"\"Session document service - creates structured session documents in SiYuan.\"\"\"\n\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\n\nfrom ies_backend.schemas.entity import ExtractionResult, ExtractedEntity\nfrom ies_backend.services.siyuan_client import SiYuanClient\n\n\nclass SessionDocumentService:\n    \"\"\"Service for creating session documents in SiYuan.\"\"\"\n\n    # Default notebook for sessions\n    DEFAULT_NOTEBOOK = \"20241201000000-ies\"  # Will be configured\n\n    def __init__(self, notebook_id: str | None = None):\n        \"\"\"Initialize with optional notebook override.\"\"\"\n        self.notebook_id = notebook_id or self.DEFAULT_NOTEBOOK\n\n    async def create_session_document(\n        self,\n        user_id: str,\n        extraction: ExtractionResult,\n        session_title: str | None = None,\n        session_date: str | None = None,\n    ) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Create a session document in SiYuan.\n\n        Args:\n            user_id: User ID\n            extraction: Extraction result with entities and summary\n            session_title: Optional title (defaults to date-based)\n            session_date: Optional date string (defaults to now)\n\n        Returns:\n            Document ID\n        \"\"\"\n        date = session_date or datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime(\"%Y-%m-%d\")\n        title = session_title or f\"Session {date}\"\n        path = f\"/Sessions/{user_id}/{date}-{title.replace(' ', '-').lower()}\"\n\n        markdown = self._render_session_document(\n            title=title,\n            date=date,\n            extraction=extraction,\n        )\n\n        result = await SiYuanClient.create_doc(\n            self.notebook_id,\n            path,\n            markdown,\n        )\n\n        return result.get(\"id\", \"\")\n\n    def _render_session_document(\n        self,\n        title: str,\n        date: str,\n        extraction: ExtractionResult,\n    ) -> str:\n        \"\"\"Render session document as markdown.\"\"\"\n        lines = [\n            f\"# {title}\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"*Date: {date}*\",\n            \"\",\n        ]\n\n        # Key Insights\n        if extraction.session_summary.key_insights:\n            lines.extend([\n                \"## Key Insights\",\n                \"\",\n            ])\n            for insight in extraction.session_summary.key_insights:\n                lines.append(f\"- {insight}\")\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        # Entities Discussed\n        if extraction.entities:\n            lines.extend([\n                \"## Entities Discussed\",\n                \"\",\n            ])\n            for entity in extraction.entities:\n                lines.extend(self._render_entity_section(entity))\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        # Open Questions\n        if extraction.session_summary.open_questions:\n            lines.extend([\n                \"## Open Questions\",\n                \"\",\n            ])\n            for question in extraction.session_summary.open_questions:\n                lines.append(f\"- {question}\")\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        # Threads Explored\n        if extraction.session_summary.threads_explored:\n            lines.extend([\n                \"## Threads Explored\",\n                \"\",\n            ])\n            for thread in extraction.session_summary.threads_explored:\n                lines.append(f\"- {thread}\")\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        # Key Quotes (from all entities)\n        all_quotes = []\n        for entity in extraction.entities:\n            for quote in entity.quotes:\n                all_quotes.append((entity.name, quote))\n\n        if all_quotes:\n            lines.extend([\n                \"## Key Quotes\",\n                \"\",\n            ])\n            for entity_name, quote in all_quotes:\n                lines.append(f\"> {quote}\")\n                lines.append(f\"> — *re: {entity_name}*\")\n                lines.append(\"\")\n\n        return \"\\n\".join(lines)\n\n    def _render_entity_section(self, entity: ExtractedEntity) -> list[str]:\n        \"\"\"Render a single entity as markdown section.\"\"\"\n        lines = [\n            f\"### {entity.name}\",\n            \"\",\n            f\"**Kind:** {entity.kind.value} | **Domain:** {entity.domain.value} | **Status:** {entity.status.value}\",\n            \"\",\n            entity.description,\n            \"\",\n        ]\n\n        if entity.connections:\n            lines.append(\"**Connections:**\")\n            for conn in entity.connections:\n                lines.append(f\"- {conn.relationship.value} → {conn.to}\")\n            lines.append(\"\")\n\n        return lines\n"

      "content": "\"\"\"Entity storage service - persists entities to Neo4j graph.\"\"\"\n\nfrom datetime import datetime, timezone\nfrom typing import Any\n\nfrom ies_backend.schemas.entity import ExtractedEntity, ExtractionResult\nfrom ies_backend.services.neo4j_client import Neo4jClient\n\n\nclass EntityStorageService:\n    \"\"\"Service for storing extracted entities in Neo4j.\"\"\"\n\n    async def store_entities(\n        self,\n        user_id: str,\n        session_id: str,\n        extraction: ExtractionResult,\n    ) -> tuple[list[str], list[str]]:\n        \"\"\"Store extracted entities in Neo4j.\n\n        Args:\n            user_id: User ID\n            session_id: Session document ID\n            extraction: Extraction result with entities\n\n        Returns:\n            Tuple of (created_entity_names, updated_entity_names)\n        \"\"\"\n        created = []\n        updated = []\n\n        for entity in extraction.entities:\n            # Check if entity exists\n            existing = await self._find_entity(user_id, entity.name)\n\n            if existing:\n                # Update existing entity\n                await self._update_entity(user_id, entity, session_id)\n                updated.append(entity.name)\n            else:\n                # Create new entity\n                await self._create_entity(user_id, entity, session_id)\n                created.append(entity.name)\n\n        # Create connections between entities\n        await self._create_connections(user_id, extraction.entities)\n\n        return created, updated\n\n    async def _find_entity(\n        self, user_id: str, entity_name: str\n    ) -> dict[str, Any] | None:\n        \"\"\"Find an entity by name for a user.\"\"\"\n        query = \"\"\"\n        MATCH (e:Entity {user_id: $user_id, name: $name})\n        RETURN e\n        \"\"\"\n        results = await Neo4jClient.execute_query(\n            query, {\"user_id\": user_id, \"name\": entity_name}\n        )\n        return results[0][\"e\"] if results else None\n\n    async def _create_entity(\n        self,\n        user_id: str,\n        entity: ExtractedEntity,\n        session_id: str,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Create a new entity node.\"\"\"\n        query = \"\"\"\n        CREATE (e:Entity {\n            user_id: $user_id,\n            name: $name,\n            kind: $kind,\n            domain: $domain,\n            status: $status,\n            description: $description,\n            quotes: $quotes,\n            created_at: $created_at,\n            updated_at: $updated_at,\n            session_ids: [$session_id]\n        })\n        \"\"\"\n        now = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()\n        await Neo4jClient.execute_write(\n            query,\n            {\n                \"user_id\": user_id,\n                \"name\": entity.name,\n                \"kind\": entity.kind.value,\n                \"domain\": entity.domain.value,\n                \"status\": entity.status.value,\n                \"description\": entity.description,\n                \"quotes\": entity.quotes,\n                \"created_at\": now,\n                \"updated_at\": now,\n                \"session_id\": session_id,\n            },\n        )\n\n    async def _update_entity(\n        self,\n        user_id: str,\n        entity: ExtractedEntity,\n        session_id: str,\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Update an existing entity node.\"\"\"\n        # Update entity, promoting status if appropriate\n        # (seed → developing → solid, never demote)\n        query = \"\"\"\n        MATCH (e:Entity {user_id: $user_id, name: $name})\n        SET e.description = $description,\n            e.updated_at = $updated_at,\n            e.quotes = e.quotes + $new_quotes,\n            e.session_ids = e.session_ids + [$session_id],\n            e.status = CASE\n                WHEN e.status = 'seed' AND $status IN ['developing', 'solid'] THEN $status\n                WHEN e.status = 'developing' AND $status = 'solid' THEN $status\n                ELSE e.status\n            END\n        \"\"\"\n        await Neo4jClient.execute_write(\n            query,\n            {\n                \"user_id\": user_id,\n                \"name\": entity.name,\n                \"description\": entity.description,\n                \"updated_at\": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),\n                \"new_quotes\": entity.quotes,\n                \"session_id\": session_id,\n                \"status\": entity.status.value,\n            },\n        )\n\n    async def _create_connections(\n        self, user_id: str, entities: list[ExtractedEntity]\n    ) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Create connections between entities.\"\"\"\n        for entity in entities:\n            for conn in entity.connections:\n                # Create relationship if target exists\n                query = \"\"\"\n                MATCH (from:Entity {user_id: $user_id, name: $from_name})\n                MATCH (to:Entity {user_id: $user_id, name: $to_name})\n                MERGE (from)-[r:RELATES_TO {type: $rel_type}]->(to)\n                ON CREATE SET r.created_at = $now\n                \"\"\"\n                await Neo4jClient.execute_write(\n                    query,\n                    {\n                        \"user_id\": user_id,\n                        \"from_name\": entity.name,\n                        \"to_name\": conn.to,\n                        \"rel_type\": conn.relationship.value,\n                        \"now\": datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat(),\n                    },\n                )\n\n    async def get_user_entities(\n        self, user_id: str, limit: int = 50\n    ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:\n        \"\"\"Get all entities for a user.\"\"\"\n        query = \"\"\"\n        MATCH (e:Entity {user_id: $user_id})\n        RETURN e\n        ORDER BY e.updated_at DESC\n        LIMIT $limit\n        \"\"\"\n        results = await Neo4jClient.execute_query(\n            query, {\"user_id\": user_id, \"limit\": limit}\n        )\n        return [r[\"e\"] for r in results]\n\n    async def get_entity_graph(\n        self, user_id: str, entity_name: str, depth: int = 2\n    ) -> dict[str, Any]:\n        \"\"\"Get an entity and its connected entities.\n\n        Args:\n            user_id: User ID\n            entity_name: Name of central entity\n            depth: How many hops to traverse\n\n        Returns:\n            Dict with entity and its connections\n        \"\"\"\n        query = \"\"\"\n        MATCH path = (e:Entity {user_id: $user_id, name: $name})-[*0..{depth}]-(connected)\n        WHERE connected:Entity\n        WITH e, collect(DISTINCT connected) as connected_entities,\n             collect(DISTINCT relationships(path)) as all_rels\n        RETURN e, connected_entities, all_rels\n        \"\"\".replace(\"{depth}\", str(depth))\n\n        results = await Neo4jClient.execute_query(\n            query, {\"user_id\": user_id, \"name\": entity_name}\n        )\n\n        if not results:\n            return {\"entity\": None, \"connected\": [], \"relationships\": []}\n\n        return {\n            \"entity\": results[0][\"e\"],\n            \"connected\": results[0][\"connected_entities\"],\n            \"relationships\": results[0][\"all_rels\"],\n        }\n"
    }
  }
]

Return summary\n\n    Args:\n        request: Session processing request with transcript and metadata\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        # 1. Extract entities\n        extraction = await extraction_service.extract_entities(request.transcript)\n\n        # 2. Create session document in SiYuan\n        session_doc_id = None\n        try:\n            session_doc_id = await document_service.create_session_document(\n                user_id=request.user_id,\n                extraction=extraction,\n                session_title=request.session_title,\n                session_date=request.session_date,\n            )\n        except Exception as e:\n            # SiYuan might not be available, continue without it\n            session_doc_id = f\"siyuan_unavailable: {str(e)}\"\n\n        # 3.     "content": "{\"result\":\"# Intelligent Exploration System - Architecture\\n\\n## Core Concept\\n\\nThe IES is an AI plugin for SiYuan that guides knowledge exploration through conversation, automatically extracting entities and connections, and building integrated understanding over time.\\n\\n**Key insight:** The user never manages metadata. They just have conversations. The AI does entity extraction, connection discovery, and pattern recognition.\\n\\n## The Exploration Loop\\n\\n```\\nSessions (Develop mode)\\n    │\\n    ├── creates ──► Entity Pages ◄──── Literature (from books)\\n    │                    │\\n    │                    ▼\\n    │              Knowledgebase (Neo4j + SiYuan)\\n    │                    │\\n    │                    │ (Explore mode)\\n    │                    ▼\\n    └── updates ──► Integrated Theories (Synthesize mode)\\n```\\n\\n## Three Artifacts Per Session\\n\\n1. **Session Document** - What happened (immutable record)\\n   - Topics explored, entities created, connections discovered\\n   - Research triggered, open questions\\n   - Links to transcript and entities\\n\\n2. **Raw Transcript** - Full conversation preserved\\n   - AI processing notes attached\\n   - Provenance for quotes\\n\\n3. **Entity Pages** - Updated/created from session\\n   - Core statement, evolution history\\n   - Connections to KB\\n   - Source quotes from sessions\\n\\n## Plugin Modes\\n\\n### Develop Mode (Socratic)\\n- AI guides with personalized questions\\n- Follows threads based on user response\\n- Identifies entities as they emerge in conversation\\n- Creates session document at end\\n- Updates entity pages and graph\\n\\n### Explore Mode\\n- Browse knowledgebase (literature + personal)\\n- Clickable entities → creates page on demand\\n- Find connections, fill gaps\\n- Queue research\\n\\n### Synthesize Mode\\n- Integrate learnings into Integrated Theory documents\\n- AI helps weave entities into coherent narrative\\n- Identifies gaps in the theory\\n\\n## Knowledgebase: Annotation Layer\\n\\n- Literature entities live in Neo4j (49k)\\n- SiYuan pages created ON DEMAND when accessed\\n- Personal entities always have pages\\n- Hub page shows: stats, recent, most connected, suggestions\\n\\n## Ontology: Flexible Properties\\n\\nInstead of rigid entity types, use block attributes:\\n- `custom-kind`: idea, person, process, artifact, etc.\\n- `custom-domain`: therapy, software, personal, etc.\\n- `custom-status`: seed, developing, solid\\n- Additional tags for enrichment\\n\\nAI identifies and applies these during extraction - user doesn't manage.\\n\\n## Session Flow\\n\\n1. User starts session (or AI suggests based on gaps)\\n2. AI guides exploration with questions\\n3. Entities identified in real-time\\n4. AI: \\\"Let me capture what emerged...\\\" → generates session doc\\n5. Graph updated, entity pages updated\\n6. Hub refreshed with new stats/suggestions\\n\"}"
  }

Transcript\n      ↓\n2. Claude API (extraction prompt)\n      ↓\n3. Parse: entities + session_summary\n      ↓\n   ┌──────────────────┐\n   │                  │\n   ▼                  ▼\n4. SiYuan         5. Neo4j\n   Session Doc       Entities\n   (markdown)        + Connections\n```\n\n### Extraction Prompt\n\nThe Claude extraction prompt asks for:\n- Entity name, kind, domain, status\n- Description\n- Exact quotes from transcript\n- Connections to other entities\n- Session summary (key insights, open questions, threads explored)\n\n---\n\n## Session Document Structure\n\nGenerated markdown document with sections:\n\n1. **Key Insights** — What emerged\n2. **Entities Discussed** — With kind/domain/status and connections\n3. **Open Questions** — Unresolved threads\n4. **Key Quotes** — Important moments with entity attribution\n\n---\n\n## API Request/Response\n\n### POST /session/process\n\n**Request:**\n```json\n{\n  \"user_id\": \"string\",\n  \"transcript\": \"string\",\n  \"session_title\": \"optional string\",\n  \"session_date\": \"optional YYYY-MM-DD\"\n}\n```\n\n**Response:**\n```json\n{\n  \"session_doc_id\": \"string\",\n  \"entities_created\": [\"entity names\"],\n  \"entities_updated\": [\"entity names\"],\n  \"summary\": {\n    \"key_insights\": [\"...\"],\n    \"open_questions\": [\"...\"],\n    \"threads_explored\": [\"...\"]\n  }\n}\n```\n\n---\n\n## Next: Phase 3\n\nThe Question Engine will implement:\n- State detection logic\n- Approach selection rules\n- Question templates from books"
